<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-104">[.NET Framework 4.7.1](#v471)  </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-104">[.NET Framework 4.7.1](#v471)  </span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-105">[.NET Framework 4.7](#v47) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-105">[.NET Framework 4.7](#v47) </span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-106">[.NET Framework 4.6.2](#v462) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-106">[.NET Framework 4.6.2](#v462) </span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-107">[.NET Framework 4.6.1](#v461) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-107">[.NET Framework 4.6.1](#v461) </span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-108">[.NET 2015 和 .NET Framework 4.6](#v46) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-108">[.NET 2015 and .NET Framework 4.6](#v46) </span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-109">[.NET Framework 4.5.2](#v452) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-109">[.NET Framework 4.5.2](#v452) </span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-110">[.NET Framework 4.5.1](#v451) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-110">[.NET Framework 4.5.1](#v451) </span></span>  
[<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-111">.NET Framework 4.5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-111">.NET Framework 4.5</span></span>](#v45)   

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-112">本文不提供有关每项新增功能的完整信息，并有可能会发生更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-112">This article does not provide comprehensive information about each new feature and is subject to change.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-113">有关 .NET Framework 的常规信息，请参阅[入门](../../../docs/framework/get-started/index.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-113">For general information about the .NET Framework, see [Getting Started](../../../docs/framework/get-started/index.md).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-114">有关支持的平台，请参阅[系统要求](~/docs/framework/get-started/system-requirements.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-114">For supported platforms, see [System Requirements](~/docs/framework/get-started/system-requirements.md).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-115">有关下载链接和安装说明，请参阅[安装指南](../../../docs/framework/install/guide-for-developers.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-115">For download links and installation instructions, see [Installation Guide](../../../docs/framework/install/guide-for-developers.md).</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-116">.NET Framework 团队还发布 NuGet 带外功能以扩展平台支持并引入新功能，如不可变集合和启用了 SIMD 的矢量类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-116">The .NET Framework team also releases features out of band with NuGet to expand platform support and to introduce new functionality, such as immutable collections and SIMD-enabled vector types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-117">有关详细信息，请参阅[其他类库和 API](../additional-apis/index.md) 以及 [.NET Framework 和带外版本](~/docs/framework/get-started/the-net-framework-and-out-of-band-releases.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-117">For more information, see [Additional Class Libraries and APIs](../additional-apis/index.md) and [The .NET Framework and Out-of-Band Releases](~/docs/framework/get-started/the-net-framework-and-out-of-band-releases.md).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-118">请参阅 .NET Framework 的 [NuGet 包的完整列表](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/p/nugetpackages/)，或订阅[我们的源](https://nuget.org/api/v2/curated-feeds/dotnetframework/Packages/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-118">See a [complete list of NuGet packages](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/p/nugetpackages/) for the .NET Framework, or subscribe to [our feed](https://nuget.org/api/v2/curated-feeds/dotnetframework/Packages/).</span></span>

<a name="v471"></a> 
## <a name="introducing-the-net-framework-471"></a><span data-ttu-id="fdea9-119">.NET Framework 4.7.1 简介</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-119">Introducing the .NET Framework 4.7.1</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-120">.NET Framework 4.7.1 在 .NET Framework 4.6、4.6.1、4.6.2 和 4.7 的基础之上构建而成，新增了许多修补程序和功能，同时很好地保持了产品的稳定性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-120">The .NET Framework 4.7.1 builds on the .NET Framework 4.6, 4.6.1, 4.6.2, and 4.7 by adding many new fixes and several new features while remaining a very stable product.</span></span>

### <a name="downloading-and-installing-the-net-framework-471"></a><span data-ttu-id="fdea9-121">下载和安装 .NET Framework 4.7.1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-121">Downloading and installing the .NET Framework 4.7.1</span></span>
 
<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-122">可以从下列位置下载 .NET Framework 4.7.1：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-122">You can download the .NET Framework 4.7.1  from the following locations:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-123">.NET Framework 4.7.1 Web 安装程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-123">.NET Framework 4.7.1 Web Installer</span></span>](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=852095)

- [<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-124">NET Framework 4.7.1 脱机安装程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-124">NET Framework 4.7.1 Offline Installer</span></span>](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=852107)

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-125">可以在 Windows 10、Windows 8.1、Windows 7 SP1 和对应的服务器平台（版本不低于 Windows Server 2008 R2 SP1）上安装 .NET Framework 4.7.1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-125">The .NET Framework 4.7.1 can be installed on Windows 10, Windows 8.1, Windows 7 SP1, and the corresponding server platforms starting with Windows Server 2008 R2 SP1.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-126">可以使用 Web 安装程序或脱机安装程序来安装 .NET Framework 4.7.1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-126">You can install the .NET Framework 4.7.1 by using either the web installer or the offline installer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-127">适用于大多数用户的建议方法是使用 Web 安装程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-127">The recommended way for most users is to use the web installer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-128">可以通过安装 [.NET Framework 4.7.1 开发人员工具包](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=852105)，在 Visual Studio 2012 或更高版本中定位 .NET Framework 4.7.1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-128">You can target the .NET Framework 4.7.1 in Visual Studio 2012 or later by installing the [.NET Framework 4.7.1 Developer Pack](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=852105).</span></span> 

### <a name="whats-new-in-the-net-framework-471"></a><span data-ttu-id="fdea9-129">.NET Framework 4.7.1 中的新增功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-129">What's new in the .NET Framework 4.7.1</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-130">.NET Framework 4.7.1 在以下几个领域新增了功能：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-130">The .NET Framework 4.7.1 includes new features in the following areas:</span></span>
 
- [<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-131">核心</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-131">Core</span></span>](#core471)
- [<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-132">公共语言运行时 (CLR)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-132">Common language runtime (CLR)</span></span>](#clr)
- [<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-133">网络连接</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-133">Networking</span></span>](#net471)
- [<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-134">ASP.NET 2.0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-134">ASP.NET</span></span>](#asp-net471) 

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-135">此外，.NET Framework 4.7.1 的重点是改进了辅助功能，使应用程序能为辅助技术的用户提供最佳体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-135">In addition, a major focus in the .NET Framework 4.7.1 is improved accessibility, which allows an application to provide an appropriate experience for users of Assistive Technology.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-136">有关 .NET Framework 4.7.1 中辅助功能改进的信息，请参阅 [.NET Framework 中辅助功能的新增功能](whats-new-in-accessibility.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-136">For information on accessibility improvements in the .NET Framework 4.7.1, see [What's new in accessibility in the .NET Framework](whats-new-in-accessibility.md).</span></span> 

<a name="core471" />
#### <a name="core"></a><span data-ttu-id="fdea9-137">核心</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-137">Core</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-138">**支持 .NET Standard 2.0**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-138">**Support for .NET Standard 2.0**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-139">[.NET Standard](~/docs/standard/net-standard.md) 定义一组 API，这些 API 必须可用于支持 Standard 版本的每个 .NET 实现。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-139">[.NET Standard](~/docs/standard/net-standard.md) defines a set of APIs that must be available on each .NET implementation that supports that version of the standard.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-140">.NET Framework 4.7.1 完全支持 .NET Standard 2.0 并增加了[ 200 个 API](https://github.com/dotnet/standard/blob/master/netstandard/src/ApiCompatBaseline.net461.txt)，这些 API 在 .NET Standard 2.0 中定义，.NET Framework 4.6.1、4.6.2 和 4.7 中也延续使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-140">The .NET Framework 4.7.1 fully supports .NET Standard 2.0 and adds [about 200 APIs](https://github.com/dotnet/standard/blob/master/netstandard/src/ApiCompatBaseline.net461.txt) that are defined in .NET Standard 2.0 and are missing from the .NET Framework 4.6.1, 4.6.2, and 4.7.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-141">（请注意，这些版本的 .NET Framework 只有在其他 .NET Standard 支持文件也部署在目标系统时才支持 .NET Standard 2.0。）有关详细信息，请参阅 [.NET Framework 4.7.1 Runtime and Compiler Features](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2017/09/28/net-framework-4-7-1-runtime-and-compiler-features)（.NET Framework 4.7.1 运行时和编译器功能）博客文章中的“BCL - .NET Standard 2.0 Support”（BCL - .NET Standard 2.0 支持）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-141">(Note that these versions of the .NET Framework support .NET Standard 2.0 only if additional .NET Standard support files are also deployed on the target system.) For more information, see "BCL - .NET Standard 2.0 Support" in the [.NET Framework 4.7.1 Runtime and Compiler Features](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2017/09/28/net-framework-4-7-1-runtime-and-compiler-features) blog post.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-142">**支持配置生成器**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-142">**Support for configuration builders**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-143">配置生成器允许开发者在运行时动态地插入和生成应用程序的配置设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-143">Configuration builders allow developers to inject and build configuration settings for applications dynamically at run time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-144">自定义配置生成器可用于修改配置节中的现有数据，也可用于生成全新的配置节。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-144">Custom configuration builders can be used to modify existing data in a configuration section or to build a configuration section entirely from scratch.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-145">如果没有配置生成器，.config 文件将是静态的，并且其设置将在应用程序启动之前定义。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-145">Without configuration builders, .config files are static, and their settings are defined some time before an application is launched.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-146">若要创建自定义配置生成器，请从抽象的 <xref:System.Configuration.ConfigurationBuilder> 类派生生成器并且替代其 <xref:System.Configuration.ConfigurationBuilder.ProcessConfigurationSection%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> 和 <xref:System.Configuration.ConfigurationBuilder.ProcessRawXml%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-146">To create a custom configuration builder, you derive your builder from the abstract <xref:System.Configuration.ConfigurationBuilder> class and override its <xref:System.Configuration.ConfigurationBuilder.ProcessConfigurationSection%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> and <xref:System.Configuration.ConfigurationBuilder.ProcessRawXml%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-147">也可在 .config 文件中定义生成器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-147">You also define your builders in your .config file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-148">有关详细信息，请参阅 [.NET Framework 4.7.1 ASP.NET and Configuration Features](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2017/09/13/net-framework-4-7-1-asp-net-and-configuration-features)（.NET Framework 4.7.1 ASP.NET 和配置功能）博客文章中的“Configuration Builders”（配置生成器）一节。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-148">For more information, see the "Configuration Builders" section in the [.NET Framework 4.7.1 ASP.NET and Configuration Features](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2017/09/13/net-framework-4-7-1-asp-net-and-configuration-features) blog post.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-149">**运行时功能检测**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-149">**Run-time feature detection**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-150"><xref:System.Runtime.CompilerServices.RuntimeFeature?displayProperty=nameWithType> 类提供一种机制，用于确定给定的 .NET 实现在编译时或运行时是否支持预定义的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-150">The <xref:System.Runtime.CompilerServices.RuntimeFeature?displayProperty=nameWithType> class provides a mechanism for determine whether a predefined feature is supported on a given .NET implementation at compile time or run time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-151">在编译时，编译器可以检查指定的字段是否存在，以确定是否支持某项功能，如果支持，它会发出利用这一功能的代码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-151">At compile time, a compiler can check whether a specified field exists to determine whether the feature is supported; if so, it can emit code that takes advantage of that feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-152">在运行时，应用程序可以在运行时发出代码之前调用 <xref:System.Runtime.CompilerServices.RuntimeFeature.IsSupported%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> 方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-152">At run time, an application can call the <xref:System.Runtime.CompilerServices.RuntimeFeature.IsSupported%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> method before emitting code at runtime.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-153">有关详细信息，请参阅 [Add helper method to describe features supported by the runtime](https://github.com/dotnet/corefx/issues/17116)（添加 helper 方法以描述运行时支持的功能）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-153">For more information, see [Add helper method to describe features supported by the runtime](https://github.com/dotnet/corefx/issues/17116).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-154">**值元组类型是可序列化的**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-154">**Value tuple types are serializable**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-155">从 .NET Framework 4.7.1 起，<xref:System.ValueTuple?displayProperty=nameWithType> 及其相关的泛型类型被标记为[可序列化](xref:System.SerializableAttribute)，允许进行二进制序列化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-155">Starting with the .NET Framework 4.7.1, <xref:System.ValueTuple?displayProperty=nameWithType> and its associated generic types are marked as [Serializable](xref:System.SerializableAttribute), which allows binary serialization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-156">这样，可以更轻松地将元组类型（如 <xref:System.Tuple%603> 和 <xref:System.Tuple%604>）迁移到值元组类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-156">This should make migrating Tuple types, such as <xref:System.Tuple%603> and <xref:System.Tuple%604>, to value tuple types easier.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-157">有关详细信息，请参阅 [.NET Framework 4.7.1 Runtime and Compiler Features](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2017/09/28/net-framework-4-7-1-runtime-and-compiler-features)（.NET Framework 4.7.1 运行时和编译器功能）博客文章中的“Compiler -- ValueTuple is Serializable”（编译器 -- 值元组是可序列化的）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-157">For more information, see "Compiler -- ValueTuple is Serializable" in the [.NET Framework 4.7.1 Runtime and Compiler Features](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2017/09/28/net-framework-4-7-1-runtime-and-compiler-features) blog post.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-158">**支持只读引用**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-158">**Support for read-only references**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-159">.NET Framework 4.7.1 增加了 <xref:System.Runtime.CompilerServices.IsReadOnlyAttribute?displayProperty=nameWithType>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-159">The .NET Framework 4.7.1 adds the <xref:System.Runtime.CompilerServices.IsReadOnlyAttribute?displayProperty=nameWithType>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-160">此特性由语言编译器用于标记具有只读 ref 返回类型或参数的成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-160">This attribute is used by language compilers to mark members that have read-only ref return types or parameters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-161">有关详细信息，请参阅 [.NET Framework 4.7.1 Runtime and Compiler Features](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2017/09/28/net-framework-4-7-1-runtime-and-compiler-features)（.NET Framework 4.7.1 运行时和编译器功能）博客文章中的“Compiler -- Support for ReadOnlyReferences”（编译器 -- 支持只读引用）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-161">For more information, see "Compiler -- Support for ReadOnlyReferences" in the [.NET Framework 4.7.1 Runtime and Compiler Features](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2017/09/28/net-framework-4-7-1-runtime-and-compiler-features) blog post.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-162">有关 ref 返回值的信息，请参阅 [ref 返回值和 ref 局部变量（C# 指南）](~/docs/csharp/programming-guide/classes-and-structs/ref-returns.md)和 [ref 返回值 (Visual Basic)](../../visual-basic/programming-guide/language-features/procedures/ref-return-values.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-162">For information on ref return values, see [Ref return values and ref locals (C# Guide)](~/docs/csharp/programming-guide/classes-and-structs/ref-returns.md) and [Ref return values (Visual Basic)](../../visual-basic/programming-guide/language-features/procedures/ref-return-values.md).</span></span>

<a name="clr" />
#### <a name="common-language-runtime-clr"></a><span data-ttu-id="fdea9-163">公共语言运行时 (CLR)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-163">Common language runtime (CLR)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-164">**垃圾回收性能改进**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-164">**Garbage collection performance improvements**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-165">.NET Framework 4.7.1 中的垃圾回收 (GC) 的更改提升了整体性能，尤其是大型对象堆 (LOH) 分配的性能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-165">Changes to garbage collection (GC) in the .NET Framework 4.7.1 improve overall performance, especially for Large Object Heap (LOH) allocations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-166">在 .NET Framework 4.7.1 中，小型对象堆 (SOH) 分配和 LOH 分配使用不同的锁，当后台 GC (BGC) 整理 SOH 时即发生 LOH 分配。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-166">In the .NET Framework 4.7.1, separate locks are used for Small Object Heap (SOH) and LOH allocations, which allows LOH allocations to occur when Background GC (BGC) is sweeping the SOH.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-167">这样，进行大量 LOH 分配的应用程序发生分配锁争用的情况将减少，从而提高性能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-167">As a result, applications that make a large number of LOH allocations should see a reduction in allocation lock contention and improved performance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-168">有关详细信息，请参阅 [.NET Framework 4.7.1 Runtime and Compiler Features](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2017/09/28/net-framework-4-7-1-runtime-and-compiler-features/)（.NET Framework 4.7.1 运行时和编译器功能）博客文章中的“Runtime -- GC Performance Improvements”（运行时 -- GC 性能改进）一节。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-168">For more information, see the "Runtime -- GC Performance Improvements" section in the [.NET Framework 4.7.1 Runtime and Compiler Features](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2017/09/28/net-framework-4-7-1-runtime-and-compiler-features/) blog post.</span></span> 

<a name="net471"/>
#### <a name="networking"></a><span data-ttu-id="fdea9-169">网络</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-169">Networking</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-170">**Message.HashAlgorithm 的 SHA-2 支持**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-170">**SHA-2 support for Message.HashAlgorithm**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-171">在 .NET Framework 4.7 及早期版本中，<xref:System.Messaging.Message.HashAlgorithm%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> 属性仅支持 <xref:System.Messaging.HashAlgorithm.Md5?displayProperty=nameWithType> 和 <xref:System.Messaging.HashAlgorithm.Sha?displayProperty=nameWithType> 的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-171">In the .NET Framework 4.7 and earlier versions, the <xref:System.Messaging.Message.HashAlgorithm%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> property supported values of <xref:System.Messaging.HashAlgorithm.Md5?displayProperty=nameWithType> and <xref:System.Messaging.HashAlgorithm.Sha?displayProperty=nameWithType> only.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-172">从 .NET Framework 4.7.1 开始，还支持 <xref:System.Messaging.HashAlgorithm.Sha256?displayProperty=nameWithType>、<xref:System.Messaging.HashAlgorithm.Sha384?displayProperty=nameWithType> 和 <xref:System.Messaging.HashAlgorithm.Sha512?displayProperty=nameWithType>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-172">Starting with the .NET Framework 4.7.1, <xref:System.Messaging.HashAlgorithm.Sha256?displayProperty=nameWithType>, <xref:System.Messaging.HashAlgorithm.Sha384?displayProperty=nameWithType>, and <xref:System.Messaging.HashAlgorithm.Sha512?displayProperty=nameWithType> are also supported.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-173">实际是否使用此值取决于消息队列，因为 <xref:System.Messaging.Message> 实例本身不进行哈希处理，而是简单地将值传递到消息队列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-173">Whether this value is actually used depends on MSMQ, since the <xref:System.Messaging.Message> instance itself does no hashing but simply passes on values to MSMQ.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-174">有关详细信息，请参阅 [.NET Framework 4.7.1 ASP.NET and Configuration Features](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2017/09/13/net-framework-4-7-1-asp-net-and-configuration-features/)（.NET Framework 4.7.1 ASP.NET 和配置功能）博客文章中的“SHA-2 support for Message.HashAlgorithm”（Message.HashAlgorithm 的 SHA-2 支持）一节。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-174">For more information, see the "SHA-2 support for Message.HashAlgorithm" section in the [.NET Framework 4.7.1 ASP.NET and Configuration features](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2017/09/13/net-framework-4-7-1-asp-net-and-configuration-features/) blog post.</span></span>

<a name="asp-net471" />
#### <a name="aspnet"></a><span data-ttu-id="fdea9-175">ASP.NET</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-175">ASP.NET</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-176">**ASP.NET 应用程序中的执行步骤**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-176">**Execution steps in ASP.NET applications**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-177">ASP.NET 处理包括 23 个事件的预定义管道中的请求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-177">ASP.NET processes requests in a predefined pipeline that includes 23 events.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-178">ASP.NET 执行每个事件处理程序作为一个执行步骤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-178">ASP.NET executes each event handler as an execution step.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-179">对于 .NET Framework 4.7 之前的 ASP.NET 版本，由于本机和托管线程之间的切换，ASP.NET 无法传送执行上下文。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-179">In versions of ASP.NET up to the .NET Framework 4.7, ASP.NET can't flow the execution context due to switching between native and managed threads.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-180">ASP.NET 有选择性地仅传送 <xref:System.Web.HttpContext>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-180">Instead, ASP.NET selectively flows only the <xref:System.Web.HttpContext>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-181">从 .NET Framework 4.7.1 开始，<xref:System.Web.HttpApplication.OnExecuteRequestStep(System.Action{System.Web.HttpContextBase,System.Action})?displayProperty=nameWithType> 方法还允许模块还原环境数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-181">Starting with the .NET Framework 4.7.1, the <xref:System.Web.HttpApplication.OnExecuteRequestStep(System.Action{System.Web.HttpContextBase,System.Action})?displayProperty=nameWithType> method also allows modules to restore ambient data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-182">此功能针对与跟踪、分析、诊断或事务（例如应用程序的执行流）相关的库。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-182">This feature is targeted at libraries concerned with tracing, profiling, diagnostics, or transactions, for example, that care about the execution flow of the application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-183">有关详细信息，请参阅 [.NET Framework 4.7.1 ASP.NET and Configuration Features](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2017/09/13/net-framework-4-7-1-asp-net-and-configuration-features)（.NET Framework 4.7.1 ASP.NET 和配置功能）博客文章的“ASP.NET Execution Step Feature”（ASP.NET 执行步骤功能）一节。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-183">For more information, see the "ASP.NET Execution Step Feature" in the [.NET Framework 4.7.1 ASP.NET and Configuration Features](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2017/09/13/net-framework-4-7-1-asp-net-and-configuration-features) blog post.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-184">**ASP.NET HttpCookie 分析**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-184">**ASP.NET HttpCookie parsing**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-185">.NET Framework 4.7.1 包括新的方法 <xref:System.Web.HttpCookie.TryParse%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>，此方法提供标准化的方式来从字符串创建 <xref:System.Web.HttpCookie> 对象，并精确分配 cookie 值（如过期日期和路径）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-185">The .NET Framework 4.7.1 includes a new method, <xref:System.Web.HttpCookie.TryParse%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>, that provides a standardized way to create an <xref:System.Web.HttpCookie> object from a string and accurately assign cookie values such as expiration date and path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-186">有关详细信息，请参阅 [.NET Framework 4.7.1 ASP.NET and Configuration Features](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2017/09/13/net-framework-4-7-1-asp-net-and-configuration-features)（.NET Framework 4.7.1 ASP.NET 和配置功能）博客文章中的“ASP.NET HttpCookie parsing”（ASP.NET HttpCookie 分析）一节。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-186">For more information, see "ASP.NET HttpCookie parsing" in the [.NET Framework 4.7.1 ASP.NET and Configuration Features](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2017/09/13/net-framework-4-7-1-asp-net-and-configuration-features) blog post.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-187">**ASP.NET 窗体身份验证凭据的 SHA-2 哈希选项**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-187">**SHA-2 hash options for ASP.NET forms authentication credentials**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-188">在 .NET Framework 4.7 及其早期版本中，ASP.NET 允许开发者使用 MD5 或 SHA1 在配置文件中存储用户凭据和哈希密码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-188">In the .NET Framework 4.7 and earlier versions, ASP.NET allowed developers to store user credentials with hashed passwords in configuration files using either MD5 or SHA1.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-189">从 .NET Framework 4.7.1 开始，ASP.NET 还支持新的安全 SHA-2 哈希选项（如 SHA256、SHA384 和 SHA512）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-189">Starting with the .NET Framework 4.7.1, ASP.NET also supports new secure SHA-2 hash options such as SHA256, SHA384, and SHA512.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-190">SHA1 保留默认值，非默认哈希算法可以在 Web 配置文件中定义。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-190">SHA1 remains the default, and a non-default hash algorithm can be defined in the web configuration file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-191">例如:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-191">For example:</span></span>

```xml
<system.web>
    <authentication mode="Forms">
        <forms loginUrl="~/login.aspx">
          <credentials passwordFormat="SHA512">
            <user name="jdoe" password="6D003E98EA1C7F04ABF8FCB375388907B7F3EE06F278DB966BE960E7CBBD103DF30CA6D61F7E7FD981B2E4E3A64D43C836A4BEDCA165C33B163E6BCDC538A664" />
          </credentials>
        </forms>
    </authentication>
</system.web>
```

### <a name="whats-new-in-the-net-framework-47"></a><span data-ttu-id="fdea9-192">.NET Framework 4.7 中的新增功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-192">What's new in the .NET Framework 4.7</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-193">.NET Framework 4.7 在以下几个领域新增了功能：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-193">The .NET Framework 4.7 includes new features in the following areas:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-197">Windows Communication Foundation (WCF)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-197">Windows Communication Foundation (WCF)</span></span>](#wcf47)
- [<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-198">Windows 窗体</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-198">Windows Forms</span></span>](#wf47)
- [<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-199">Windows Presentation Foundation (WPF)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-199">Windows Presentation Foundation (WPF)</span></span>](#WPF47)

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-200">有关 .NET Framework 4.7 中新增 API 的列表，请参阅 GitHub 上的 [.NET Framework 4.7 API 更改](https://github.com/Microsoft/dotnet/blob/master/releases/net47/dotnet47-api-changes.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-200">For a list of new APIs added to the .NET Framework 4.7, see [.NET Framework 4.7 API Changes](https://github.com/Microsoft/dotnet/blob/master/releases/net47/dotnet47-api-changes.md) on GitHub.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-201">有关 .NET Framework 4.7 中功能改进和 bug 修复的列表，请参阅 GitHub 上的 [.NET Framework 4.7 更改列表](http://github.com/Microsoft/dotnet/blob/master/releases/net47/dotnet47-changes.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-201">For a list of feature improvements and bug fixes in the .NET Framework 4.7, see [.NET Framework 4.7 List of Changes](http://github.com/Microsoft/dotnet/blob/master/releases/net47/dotnet47-changes.md) on GitHub.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-202">有关其他信息，请参阅 .NET 博客中的 [Announcing the .NET Framework 4.7](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2017/04/05/announcing-the-net-framework-4-7/)（宣布 .NET Framework 4.7）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-202">For additional information, see [Announcing the .NET Framework 4.7](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2017/04/05/announcing-the-net-framework-4-7/) in the .NET blog.</span></span>

<a name="Core47" />
#### <a name="core"></a><span data-ttu-id="fdea9-203">核心</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-203">Core</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-204">.NET Framework 4.7 通过 <xref:System.Runtime.Serialization.Json.DataContractJsonSerializer> 改进了序列化：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-204">The .NET Framework 4.7 improves serialization by the <xref:System.Runtime.Serialization.Json.DataContractJsonSerializer>:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-205">**借助椭圆曲线加密 (ECC) 增强了功能**\*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-205">**Enhanced functionality with Elliptic Curve Cryptography (ECC)**\*</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-206">在 .NET Framework 4.7 中，`ImportParameters(ECParameters)` 方法已添加到 <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.ECDsa> 和 <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.ECDiffieHellman> 类，以允许对象表示已经建立的密钥。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-206">In the .NET Framework 4.7, `ImportParameters(ECParameters)` methods were added to the <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.ECDsa> and <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.ECDiffieHellman> classes to allow for an object to represent an already-established key.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-207">此外，还添加了 `ExportParameters(Boolean)` 方法，以便于使用显式曲线参数导出密钥。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-207">An `ExportParameters(Boolean)` method was also added for exporting the key using explicit curve parameters.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-208">.NET Framework 4.7 现已开始支持其他曲线（其中包括 Brainpool 曲线套件），并添加了预定义的定义，以便于通过新工厂方法 <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.ECDsa.Create%2A> 和 <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.ECDiffieHellman.Create%2A> 简化创建操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-208">The .NET Framework 4.7 also adds support for additional curves (including the Brainpool curve suite), and has added predefined definitions for ease-of-creation through the new <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.ECDsa.Create%2A> and <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.ECDiffieHellman.Create%2A> factory methods.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-209">有关 [.NET Framework 4.7 加密改进示例](https://gist.github.com/richlander/5a182899895a87a296c21ada97f7a54e)，请访问 GitHub。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-209">You can see an [example of .NET Framework 4.7 cryptography improvements](https://gist.github.com/richlander/5a182899895a87a296c21ada97f7a54e) on GitHub.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-210">**通过 DataContractJsonSerializer 提供更出色的控制字符支持**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-210">**Better support for control characters by the DataContractJsonSerializer**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-211">在 .NET Framework 4.7 中，<xref:System.Runtime.Serialization.Json.DataContractJsonSerializer> 串行化符合 ECMAScript 6 标准的控制字符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-211">In the .NET Framework 4.7, the <xref:System.Runtime.Serialization.Json.DataContractJsonSerializer> serializes control characters in conformity with the ECMAScript 6 standard.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-212">定位 .NET Framework 4.7 的应用程序默认启用此行为，而对于在 .NET Framework 4.7 控制下运行，但定位的是旧版 .NET Framework 的应用程序来说，这就是一项选择启用功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-212">This behavior is enabled by default for applications that target the .NET Framework 4.7, and is an opt-in feature for applications that are running under the .NET Framework 4.7 but target a previous version of the .NET Framework.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-213">有关详细信息，请参阅 [.NET Framework 4.7 中的重定目标更改](../../../docs/framework/migration-guide/retargeting-changes-in-the-net-framework-4-7.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-213">For more information, see [Retargeting Changes in the .NET Framework 4.7](../../../docs/framework/migration-guide/retargeting-changes-in-the-net-framework-4-7.md).</span></span>

<a name="net47" />
#### <a name="networking"></a><span data-ttu-id="fdea9-214">网络</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-214">Networking</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-215">.NET Framework 4.7 新增了以下网络相关功能：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-215">The .NET Framework 4.7 adds the following network-related feature:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-216">**提供对 TLS 协议的默认操作系统支持**\*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-216">**Default operating system support for TLS protocols**\*</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-217">借助 <xref:System.Net.Security.SslStream?displayProperty=nameWithType> 和上托堆栈组件（如 HTTP、FTP 和 SMTP）使用的 TLS 堆栈，开发者可以使用操作系统支持的默认 TLS 协议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-217">The TLS stack, which is used by <xref:System.Net.Security.SslStream?displayProperty=nameWithType> and up-stack components such as HTTP, FTP, and SMTP, allows developers to use the default TLS protocols supported by the operating system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-218">开发者再也不需要对 TLS 版本进行硬编码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-218">Developers need no longer hard-code a TLS version.</span></span>

<a name="ASP-NET47" />
#### <a name="aspnet"></a><span data-ttu-id="fdea9-219">ASP.NET</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-219">ASP.NET</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-220">在 .NET Framework 4.7 中，ASP.NET 新增了以下功能：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-220">In the .NET Framework 4.7, ASP.NET includes the following new features:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-221">**对象缓存扩展性**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-221">**Object Cache Extensibility**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-222">自 .NET Framework 4.7 起，ASP.NET 新增了一组 API，以便开发者可以替换内存中对象缓存和内存监视的默认 ASP.NET 实现代码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-222">Starting with the .NET Framework 4.7, ASP.NET adds a new set of APIs that allow developers to replace the default ASP.NET implementations for in-memory object caching and memory monitoring.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-223">现在，如果 ASP.NET 实现代码不充分，开发者可以替换以下三个组件中的任意一个：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-223">Developers can now replace any of the following three components if the ASP.NET implementation is not adequate:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-224">**对象缓存存储**：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-224">**Object Cache Store**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-225">在新的缓存提供程序配置部分中，开发者可以使用新接口 **ICacheStoreProvider** 为 ASP.NET 应用程序插入对象缓存的新实现代码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-225">By using the new cache providers configuration section, developers can plug in new implementations of an object cache for an ASP.NET application by using the new **ICacheStoreProvider** interface.</span></span>
 
- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-226">**内存监视**：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-226">**Memory monitoring**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-227">当运行的应用程序接近所配置的专用字节进程限制，或计算机的可用总物理内存不足时，ASP.NET 中的默认内存监视器就会通知应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-227">The default memory monitor in ASP.NET notifies applications when they are running close to the configured private bytes limit for the process, or when the machine is low on total available physical RAM.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-228">接近这些限制时，就会触发通知。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-228">When these limits are near, notifications are fired.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-229">对于某些应用程序，通知的触发点与限制过近，无法及时响应。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-229">For some applications, notifications are fired too close to the configured limits to allow for useful reactions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-230">开发人员现在可以编写自己的内存监视器，以通过使用 <xref:System.Web.Hosting.ApplicationMonitors.MemoryMonitor%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> 属性替换默认的内存监视器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-230">Developers can now write their own memory monitors to replace the default by using the <xref:System.Web.Hosting.ApplicationMonitors.MemoryMonitor%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> property.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-231">**内存限制响应**：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-231">**Memory Limit Reactions**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-232">默认情况下，当接近专用字节进程限制时，ASP.NET 会尝试释放对象缓存，并定期调用 <xref:System.GC.Collect%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-232">By default, ASP.NET attempts to trim the object cache and periodically call <xref:System.GC.Collect%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> when the private byte process limit is near.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-233">对于某些应用程序，<xref:System.GC.Collect%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> 调用频率或缓存释放量的效率低下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-233">For some applications, the frequency of calls to <xref:System.GC.Collect%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> or the amount of cache that is trimmed are inefficient.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-234">开发者现在可以向应用程序的内存监视器添加 **IObserver** 实现代码，从而替换或补充默认行为。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-234">Developers can now replace or supplement the default behavior by subscribing **IObserver** implementations to the application's memory monitor.</span></span>

<a name="wcf47" />
#### <a name="windows-communication-foundation-wcf"></a><span data-ttu-id="fdea9-235">Windows Communication Foundation (WCF)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-235">Windows Communication Foundation (WCF)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-236">Windows Communication Foundation (WCF) 新增了以下功能和更改：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-236">Windows Communication Foundation (WCF) adds the following features and changes:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-237">**能够配置 TLS 1.1 或 TLS 1.2 默认消息安全设置**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-237">**Ability to configure the default message security settings to TLS 1.1 or TLS 1.2**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-238">自 .NET Framework 4.7 起，除了 SSL 3.0 和 TLS 1.0 外，WCF 还允许配置 TLS 1.1 或 TLS 1.2 作为默认消息安全协议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-238">Starting with the .NET Framework 4.7, WCF allows you to configure TSL 1.1 or TLS 1.2 in addition to SSL 3.0 and TSL 1.0 as the default message security protocol.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-239">这是一项选择启用设置；必须向应用程序配置文件添加以下条目，才能启用此设置：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-239">This is an opt-in setting; to enable it, you must add the following entry to your application configuration file:</span></span>

```xml
<runtime>
   <AppContextSwitchOverrides value="Switch.System.ServiceModel.DisableUsingServicePointManagerSecurityProtocols=false;Switch.System.Net.DontEnableSchUseStrongCrypto=false" /> 
</runtime>
```

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-240">**提升了 WCF 应用程序和 WCF 序列化的可靠性**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-240">**Improved reliability of WCF applications and WCF serialization**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-241">WCF 包含大量代码更改，消除了争用条件，从而提升了序列化选项的性能和可靠性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-241">WCF includes a number of code changes that eliminate race conditions, thereby improving performance and the reliability of serialization options.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-242">其中包括:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-242">These include:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-243">更好地支持在调用 **SocketConnection.BeginRead** 和 **SocketConnection.Read** 时混合异步和同步代码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-243">Better support for mixing asynchronous and synchronous code in calls to **SocketConnection.BeginRead** and **SocketConnection.Read**.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-244">提升了在中止与 **SharedConnectionListener** 和 **DuplexChannelBinder** 的连接时的可靠性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-244">Improved reliability when aborting a connection with **SharedConnectionListener** and **DuplexChannelBinder**.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-245">提高了调用 <xref:System.Runtime.Serialization.FormatterServices.GetSerializableMembers%28System.Type%29?displayProperty=nameWithType> 方法时序列化操作的可靠性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-245">Improved reliability of serialization operations when calling the <xref:System.Runtime.Serialization.FormatterServices.GetSerializableMembers%28System.Type%29?displayProperty=nameWithType> method.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-246">提升了在调用 **ChannelSynchronizer.RemoveWaiter** 方法以删除等待程序时的可靠性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-246">Improved reliability when removing a waiter by calling the **ChannelSynchronizer.RemoveWaiter** method.</span></span>

<a name="wf47" />
#### <a name="windows-forms"></a><span data-ttu-id="fdea9-247">Windows 窗体</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-247">Windows Forms</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-248">在 .NET Framework 4.7 中，Windows 窗体改进了对高 DPI 监视器的支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-248">In the .NET Framework 4.7, Windows Forms improves support for high DPI monitors.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-249">**高 DPI 支持**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-249">**High DPI support**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-250">自定位 .NET Framework 4.7 的应用程序起，.NET Framework 为 Windows 窗体应用程序提供高 DPI 和动态 DPI 支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-250">Starting with applications that target the .NET Framework 4.7, the .NET Framework features high DPI and dynamic DPI support for Windows Forms applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-251">高 DPI 支持改进了高 DPI 监视器上窗体和控件的布局和外观。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-251">High DPI support improves the layout and appearance of forms and controls on high DPI monitors.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-252">当用户更改正在运行的应用程序的 DPI 或显示比例系数时，动态 DPI 会更改窗体和控件的布局和外观。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-252">Dynamic DPI changes the layout and appearance of forms and controls when the user changes the DPI or display scale factor of a running application.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-253">高 DPI 支持是一项选择启用功能，配置方法为在应用程序配置文件中定义 [\<System.Windows.Forms.ConfigurationSection>](../configure-apps/file-schema/winforms/index.md) 部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-253">High DPI support is an opt-in feature that you configure by defining a [\<System.Windows.Forms.ConfigurationSection>](../configure-apps/file-schema/winforms/index.md) section in your application configuration file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-254">若要详细了解如何向 Windows 窗体应用程序添加高 DPI 支持和动态 DPI 支持，请参阅 [Windows 窗体中的高 DPI 支持](../winforms/high-dpi-support-in-windows-forms.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-254">For more information on adding high DPI support and dynamic DPI support to your Windows Forms application, see [High DPI Support in Windows Forms](../winforms/high-dpi-support-in-windows-forms.md).</span></span>

<a name="WPF47"></a> 
#### <a name="windows-presentation-foundation-wpf"></a><span data-ttu-id="fdea9-255">Windows Presentation Foundation (WPF)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-255">Windows Presentation Foundation (WPF)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-256">在 .NET Framework 4.7 中，WPF 新增了以下增强功能：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-256">In the .NET Framework 4.7, WPF includes the following enhancements:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-257">**支持基于 Windows WM_POINTER 消息的触控/触笔堆栈**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-257">**Support for a touch/stylus stack based on Windows WM_POINTER messages**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-258">现在可以视情况使用基于 [WM_POINTER 消息](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/windows/desktop/hh454903.aspx)的触控/触笔堆栈，而不使用 Windows Ink 服务平台 (WISP)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-258">You now have the option of using a touch/stylus stack based on [WM_POINTER messages](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/windows/desktop/hh454903.aspx) instead of the Windows Ink Services Platform (WISP).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-259">这是 .NET Framework 中的一项选择启用功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-259">This is an opt-in feature in the .NET Framework.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-260">有关详细信息，请参阅 [.NET Framework 4.7 中的重定目标更改](../migration-guide/retargeting-changes-in-the-net-framework-4-7.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-260">For more information, see [Retargeting Changes in the .NET Framework 4.7](../migration-guide/retargeting-changes-in-the-net-framework-4-7.md).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-261">**WPF 打印 API 的新实现代码**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-261">**New implementation for WPF printing APIs**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-262"><xref:System.Printing.PrintQueue?displayProperty=nameWithType> 类中的 WPF 打印 API 调用 Windows [打印文档包 API](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/windows/desktop/hh448418(v=vs.85).aspx)，而不调用弃用的 [XPS 打印 API](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/windows/desktop/ff686814(v=vs.85).aspx)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-262">WPF's printing APIs in the <xref:System.Printing.PrintQueue?displayProperty=nameWithType> class call the Windows [Print Document Package API](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/windows/desktop/hh448418(v=vs.85).aspx) instead of the deprecated [XPS Print API](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/windows/desktop/ff686814(v=vs.85).aspx).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-263">若要了解此更改对应用程序兼容性造成的影响，请参阅 [.NET Framework 4.7 中的重定目标更改](../migration-guide/retargeting-changes-in-the-net-framework-4-7.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-263">For the impact of this change on application compatibility, see [Retargeting Changes in the .NET Framework 4.7](../migration-guide/retargeting-changes-in-the-net-framework-4-7.md).</span></span>

<a name="ASPNET462"></a> 
### <a name="aspnet"></a><span data-ttu-id="fdea9-279">ASP.NET</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-279">ASP.NET</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-280">在 [!INCLUDE[net_v462](../../../includes/net-v462-md.md)] 中，ASP.NET 包括以下增强功能：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-280">In the [!INCLUDE[net_v462](../../../includes/net-v462-md.md)], ASP.NET includes the following enhancements:</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-281">**改进了对数据注释验证程序中本地化错误消息的支持** 借助数据注释验证程序，能够通过将一个或多个特性添加到类属性来执行验证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-281">**Improved support for localized error messages in data annotation validators** Data annotation validators enable you to perform validation by adding one or more attributes to a class property.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-282">如果验证失败，该属性的 <xref:System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations.ValidationAttribute.ErrorMessage%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> 元素定义错误消息的文本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-282">The attribute's <xref:System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations.ValidationAttribute.ErrorMessage%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> element defines the text of the error message if validation fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-283">从 [!INCLUDE[net_v462](../../../includes/net-v462-md.md)] 开始，ASP.NET 可以轻松地本地化错误消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-283">Starting with the [!INCLUDE[net_v462](../../../includes/net-v462-md.md)], ASP.NET makes it easy to localize error messages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-284">如果有以下情况，将本地化错误消息：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-284">Error messages will be localized if:</span></span>

1.  <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-285">验证属性中提供 <xref:System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations.ValidationAttribute.ErrorMessage%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-285">The <xref:System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations.ValidationAttribute.ErrorMessage%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> is provided in the validation attribute.</span></span>

2.  <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-286">资源文件存储在 App_LocalResources 文件夹中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-286">The resource file is stored in the App_LocalResources folder.</span></span>

3.  <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-287">本地化资源文件名称的格式为 `DataAnnotation.Localization.{`*name*`}.resx`，其中 *name* 是采用 *languageCode*`-`*country/regionCode* 或 *languageCode* 格式的区域性名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-287">The name of the localized resources file has the form `DataAnnotation.Localization.{`*name*`}.resx`, where *name* is a culture name in the format *languageCode*`-`*country/regionCode* or *languageCode*.</span></span>

4.  <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-288">该资源的项名称是分配给 <xref:System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations.ValidationAttribute.ErrorMessage%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> 属性的字符串，其值是本地化的错误消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-288">The key name of the resource is the string assigned to the <xref:System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations.ValidationAttribute.ErrorMessage%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> attribute,  and its value is the localized error message.</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-289">例如，以下数据注释属性定义无效分级的默认区域性错误消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-289">For example, the following data annotation attribute defines the default culture's error message for an invalid rating.</span></span>

```csharp
public class RatingInfo
{
   [Required(ErrorMessage = "The rating must be between 1 and 10.")]
   [Display(Name = "Your Rating")]
   public int Rating { get; set; }
}
```

```vb
Public Class RatingInfo
   <Required(ErrorMessage = "The rating must be between 1 and 10.")>
   <Display(Name = "Your Rating")>
   Public Property Rating As Integer = 1
End Class
```

 <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-290">然后可以创建一个资源文件 DataAnnotation.Localization.fr.resx，它的键为错误消息字符串，值为本地化的错误消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-290">You can then create a resource file, DataAnnotation.Localization.fr.resx, whose key is the error message string and whose value is the localized error message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-291">该文件必须位于 `App.LocalResources` 文件夹中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-291">The file must be found in the `App.LocalResources` folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-292">例如，下面列出了键以及它在本地化法语 (fr) 错误消息中的值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-292">For example, the following is the key and its value in a localized French (fr) language error message:</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-293">name</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-293">Name</span></span>                                 | <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-294">“值”</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-294">Value</span></span>                                     |
| ------------------------------------ | ----------------------------------------- |
| <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-295">分级必须介于 1 和 10 之间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-295">The rating must be between 1 and 10.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-296">La note doit être comprise entre 1 et 10.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-296">La note doit être comprise entre 1 et 10.</span></span> |

 <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-297">然后，此文件可以</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-297">This file can then</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-298">此外，数据批注本地化可扩展。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-298">In addition, data annotation localization is extensible.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-299">开发人员可以通过实现 <xref:System.Web.Globalization.IStringLocalizerProvider> 接口插入自己的字符串本地化工具提供程序，以将本地化字符串存储在资源文件以外的某个位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-299">Developers can plug in their own string localizer provider by implementing the <xref:System.Web.Globalization.IStringLocalizerProvider> interface to store localization string somewhere other than in a resource file.</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-300">**会话状态存储提供程序的异步支持** ASP.NET 现允许将返回任务的方法与会话状态存储提供程序一起使用，从而使 ASP.NET 应用能够获取异步的可伸缩性优势。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-300">**Async support with session-state store providers** ASP.NET now allows task-returning methods to be used with session-state store providers, thereby allowing ASP.NET apps to get the scalability benefits of async.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-301">要使用会话状态存储提供程序支持异步操作，ASP.NET 包括一个新的接口 <xref:System.Web.SessionState.ISessionStateModule?displayProperty=nameWithType>，它继承自 <xref:System.Web.IHttpModule> 并允许开发人员实现其自己的会话状态模块和异步会话存储提供程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-301">To supports asynchronous operations with session state store providers, ASP.NET includes  a new interface, <xref:System.Web.SessionState.ISessionStateModule?displayProperty=nameWithType>, which inherits from <xref:System.Web.IHttpModule> and allows developers to implement their own session-state module and async session store providers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-302">接口定义如下：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-302">The interface is defined as follows:</span></span>

```csharp
public interface ISessionStateModule : IHttpModule {
    void ReleaseSessionState(HttpContext context);
    Task ReleaseSessionStateAsync(HttpContext context);
}
```

 <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-303">此外，<xref:System.Web.SessionState.SessionStateUtility> 类包括两种新方法：<xref:System.Web.SessionState.SessionStateUtility.IsSessionStateReadOnly%2A> 和 <xref:System.Web.SessionState.SessionStateUtility.IsSessionStateRequired%2A>，可用来支持异步操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-303">In addition, the <xref:System.Web.SessionState.SessionStateUtility> class includes two new methods, <xref:System.Web.SessionState.SessionStateUtility.IsSessionStateReadOnly%2A> and <xref:System.Web.SessionState.SessionStateUtility.IsSessionStateRequired%2A>, that can be used to support asynchronous operations.</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-304">**输出缓存提供程序的异步支持** 从 [!INCLUDE[net_v462](../../../includes/net-v462-md.md)] 开始，返回任务的方法可以与输出缓存提供程序一起使用，从而提供异步的可伸缩性优势。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-304">**Async support for output-cache providers** Starting with the [!INCLUDE[net_v462](../../../includes/net-v462-md.md)], task-returning methods can be used with output-cache providers to provide the scalability benefits of async.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-305">实现这些方法的提供程序减少了 Web 服务器上的线程阻止，并提高 ASP.NET 服务的可伸缩性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-305">Providers that implement these methods reduce thread-blocking on a web server and improve the scalability of an ASP.NET service.</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-306">添加了以下 API 以支持异步输出缓存提供程序：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-306">The following APIs have been added to support asynchronous output-cache providers:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-307"><xref:System.Web.Caching.OutputCacheProviderAsync?displayProperty=nameWithType> 类，它继承自 <xref:System.Web.Caching.OutputCacheProvider?displayProperty=nameWithType>，并允许开发人员实现异步输出缓存提供程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-307">The <xref:System.Web.Caching.OutputCacheProviderAsync?displayProperty=nameWithType> class, which inherits from <xref:System.Web.Caching.OutputCacheProvider?displayProperty=nameWithType> and allows developers to implement an asynchronous output-cache provider.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-308"><xref:System.Web.Caching.OutputCacheUtility> 类，该类提供用于配置输出缓存的 Helper 方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-308">The <xref:System.Web.Caching.OutputCacheUtility> class, which provides helper methods for configuring the output cache.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-309"><xref:System.Web.HttpCachePolicy?displayProperty=nameWithType> 类中的 18 种新方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-309">18 new methods in the
