<a name="v45"></a> 
## <a name="whats-new-in-the-net-framework-45"></a><span data-ttu-id="fdea9-857">.NET Framework 4.5 中的新增功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-857">What's new in the .NET Framework 4.5</span></span>

### <a name="core-new-features-and-improvements"></a><span data-ttu-id="fdea9-858">核心新功能和改进</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-858">Core new features and improvements</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-859">能够在部署期间通过检测并关闭 .NET Framework 4 应用程序来减少系统重启。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-859">Ability to reduce system restarts by detecting and closing .NET Framework 4 applications during deployment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-860">请参阅[在 .NET Framework 4.5 安装期间减少系统重新启动](../../../docs/framework/deployment/reducing-system-restarts.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-860">See [Reducing System Restarts During .NET Framework 4.5 Installations](../../../docs/framework/deployment/reducing-system-restarts.md).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-861">支持 64 位平台上大于 2 GB 的数组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-861">Support for arrays that are larger than 2 gigabytes (GB) on 64-bit platforms.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-862">此功能可在应用程序配置文件中启用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-862">This feature can be enabled in the application configuration file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-863">请参阅 [\<gcAllowVeryLargeObjects> 元素](../../../docs/framework/configure-apps/file-schema/runtime/gcallowverylargeobjects-element.md)，它还列出了对对象大小和数组大小的其他限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-863">See the [\<gcAllowVeryLargeObjects> element](../../../docs/framework/configure-apps/file-schema/runtime/gcallowverylargeobjects-element.md), which also lists other restrictions on object size and array size.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-864">通过服务器的后台垃圾回收来改进性能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-864">Better performance through background garbage collection for servers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-865">当你使用 [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] 中的服务器垃圾回收功能时，将自动启用后台垃圾回收。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-865">When you use server garbage collection in the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)], background garbage collection is automatically enabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-866">请参阅[垃圾回收的基础](../../../docs/standard/garbage-collection/fundamentals.md)主题的“后台服务器垃圾回收”一节。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-866">See the Background Server Garbage Collection section of the [Fundamentals of Garbage Collection](../../../docs/standard/garbage-collection/fundamentals.md) topic.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-867">后台实时 (JIT) 编译，可在多核处理器上使用此功能改进应用程序性能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-867">Background just-in-time (JIT) compilation, which is optionally available on multi-core processors to improve application performance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-868">请参阅 <xref:System.Runtime.ProfileOptimization>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-868">See <xref:System.Runtime.ProfileOptimization>.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-869">可以限制正则表达式引擎在超时之前持续尝试解析正则表达式的时间。请参阅 <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.Regex.MatchTimeout%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> 属性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-869">Ability to limit how long the regular expression engine will attempt to resolve a regular expression before it times out. See the <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.Regex.MatchTimeout%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> property.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-870">定义应用程序域的默认区域性的能力。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-870">Ability to define the default culture for an application domain.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-871">请参阅 <xref:System.Globalization.CultureInfo> 类。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-871">See the <xref:System.Globalization.CultureInfo> class.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-872">Unicode (UTF-16) 编码的控制台支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-872">Console support for Unicode (UTF-16) encoding.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-873">请参阅 <xref:System.Console> 类。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-873">See the <xref:System.Console> class.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-874">支持对区域性字符串排序和比较数据进行版本控制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-874">Support for versioning of cultural string ordering and comparison data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-875">请参阅 <xref:System.Globalization.SortVersion> 类。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-875">See the <xref:System.Globalization.SortVersion> class.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-876">改进检索资源时的性能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-876">Better performance when retrieving resources.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-877">请参阅[打包和部署资源](../../../docs/framework/resources/packaging-and-deploying-resources-in-desktop-apps.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-877">See [Packaging and Deploying Resources](../../../docs/framework/resources/packaging-and-deploying-resources-in-desktop-apps.md).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-878">Zip 压缩改进，可减少压缩文件的大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-878">Zip compression improvements to reduce the size of a compressed file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-879">请参阅 <xref:System.IO.Compression?displayProperty=nameWithType> 命名空间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-879">See the <xref:System.IO.Compression?displayProperty=nameWithType> namespace.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-880">可以通过 <xref:System.Reflection.Context.CustomReflectionContext> 类自定义用于重写默认反射行为的反射上下文。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-880">Ability to customize a reflection context to override default reflection behavior through the <xref:System.Reflection.Context.CustomReflectionContext> class.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-881">支持应用程序的国际域名 (IDNA) 标准的 2008 版（在 <xref:System.Globalization.IdnMapping?displayProperty=nameWithType> 上使用 [!INCLUDE[win8](../../../includes/win8-md.md)] 类时）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-881">Support for the 2008 version of the Internationalized Domain Names in Applications (IDNA) standard when the <xref:System.Globalization.IdnMapping?displayProperty=nameWithType> class is used  on [!INCLUDE[win8](../../../includes/win8-md.md)].</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-882">可以在 [!INCLUDE[win8](../../../includes/win8-md.md)] 使用 .NET Framework 时，将字符串比较委托给操作系统（这将实现 Unicode 6.0）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-882">Delegation of string comparison to the operating system, which implements Unicode 6.0, when the .NET Framework is used on [!INCLUDE[win8](../../../includes/win8-md.md)].</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-883">在其他平台上运行时，.NET Framework 包括其自己的字符串比较数据，这将实现 Unicode 5.x。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-883">When running on other platforms, the .NET Framework includes its own string comparison data, which implements Unicode 5.x.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-884">请参阅 <xref:System.String> 类和 <xref:System.Globalization.SortVersion> 类的“备注”部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-884">See the <xref:System.String> class and the Remarks section of the <xref:System.Globalization.SortVersion> class.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-885">能够为每个应用程序域计算字符串的哈希代码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-885">Ability to compute the hash codes for strings on a per application domain basis.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-886">请参阅 [\<UseRandomizedStringHashAlgorithm> 元素](../../../docs/framework/configure-apps/file-schema/runtime/userandomizedstringhashalgorithm-element.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-886">See [\<UseRandomizedStringHashAlgorithm> Element](../../../docs/framework/configure-apps/file-schema/runtime/userandomizedstringhashalgorithm-element.md).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-887">类型反射支持 <xref:System.Type> 和 <xref:System.Reflection.TypeInfo> 类之间的拆分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-887">Type reflection support split between <xref:System.Type> and <xref:System.Reflection.TypeInfo> classes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-888">请参阅 [.NET Framework 中用于 Windows 应用商店应用的反射](../../../docs/framework/reflection-and-codedom/reflection-for-windows-store-apps.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-888">See [Reflection in the .NET Framework for Windows Store Apps](../../../docs/framework/reflection-and-codedom/reflection-for-windows-store-apps.md).</span></span>

### <a name="managed-extensibility-framework-mef"></a><span data-ttu-id="fdea9-889">Managed Extensibility Framework (MEF)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-889">Managed Extensibility Framework (MEF)</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-890">在 [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] 中，Managed Extensibility Framework (MEF) 提供了以下新功能：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-890">In the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)], the Managed Extensibility Framework (MEF) provides the following new features:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-891">对泛型类型的支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-891">Support for generic types.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-892">利用基于约定的编程模型，你可以基于命名约定而非特性创建各个部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-892">Convention-based programming model that enables you to create parts based on naming conventions rather than attributes.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-893">多个范围。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-893">Multiple scopes.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-894">创建 [!INCLUDE[win8_appname_long](../../../includes/win8-appname-long-md.md)]应用程序时可使用的 MEF 子集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-894">A subset of MEF that you can use when you create [!INCLUDE[win8_appname_long](../../../includes/win8-appname-long-md.md)] apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-895">此子集可作为 NuGet 库中的[可下载程序包](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=256238)提供。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-895">This subset is available as a [downloadable package](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=256238) from the NuGet Gallery.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-896">若要安装此程序包，请在 Visual Studio 中打开项目，从“项目”菜单中选择“管理 NuGet 包”，然后联机搜索 `Microsoft.Composition` 程序包。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-896">To install the package, open your project in Visual Studio, choose **Manage NuGet Packages** from the **Project** menu, and search online for the `Microsoft.Composition` package.</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-897">有关详细信息，请参阅 [Managed Extensibility Framework (MEF)](../../../docs/framework/mef/index.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-897">For more information, see [Managed Extensibility Framework (MEF)](../../../docs/framework/mef/index.md).</span></span>

### <a name="asynchronous-file-operations"></a><span data-ttu-id="fdea9-898">异步文件操作</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-898">Asynchronous file operations</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-899">在 [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] 中，已将新的异步功能添加到 C# 和 Visual Basic 语言中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-899">In the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)], new asynchronous features were added to the C# and Visual Basic languages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-900">这些功能将添加用于执行异步操作的基于任务的模型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-900">These features add a task-based model for performing asynchronous operations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-901">若要使用此新模型，请使用 I/O 类中的异步方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-901">To use this new model, use the asynchronous methods in the I/O classes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-902">请参阅[异步文件 I/O](../../../docs/standard/io/asynchronous-file-i-o.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-902">See [Asynchronous File I/O](../../../docs/standard/io/asynchronous-file-i-o.md).</span></span>

<a name="tools"></a> 
### <a name="tools"></a><span data-ttu-id="fdea9-903">工具</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-903">Tools</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-904">在 [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] 中，资源文件生成器 (Resgen.exe) 使你可以从嵌入 .NET Framework 程序集中的 .resources 文件中创建用于 [!INCLUDE[win8_appname_long](../../../includes/win8-appname-long-md.md)]应用程序的 .resw 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-904">In the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)], Resource File Generator (Resgen.exe) enables you to create a .resw file for use in [!INCLUDE[win8_appname_long](../../../includes/win8-appname-long-md.md)] apps from a .resources file embedded in a .NET Framework assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-905">有关详细信息，请参阅 [Resgen.exe（资源文件生成器）](../../../docs/framework/tools/resgen-exe-resource-file-generator.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-905">For more information, see [Resgen.exe (Resource File Generator)](../../../docs/framework/tools/resgen-exe-resource-file-generator.md).</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-906">利用按托管配置优化 (Mpgo.exe) 工具，你可以通过优化本机映像程序集来改进应用程序的启动时间、内存使用率（工作集大小）和吞吐量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-906">Managed Profile Guided Optimization (Mpgo.exe) enables you to improve application startup time, memory utilization (working set size), and throughput by optimizing native image assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-907">该命令行工具会针对本机映像应用程序程序集生成配置文件数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-907">The command-line tool generates profile data for native image application assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-908">请参阅 [Mpgo.exe（按托管配置文件优化工具）](../../../docs/framework/tools/mpgo-exe-managed-profile-guided-optimization-tool.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-908">See [Mpgo.exe (Managed Profile Guided Optimization Tool)](../../../docs/framework/tools/mpgo-exe-managed-profile-guided-optimization-tool.md).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-909">从 [!INCLUDE[vs_dev12](../../../includes/vs-dev12-md.md)] 开始，可以使用 Mpgo.exe 优化 [!INCLUDE[win8_appname_long](../../../includes/win8-appname-long-md.md)]应用程序以及桌面应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-909">Starting with [!INCLUDE[vs_dev12](../../../includes/vs-dev12-md.md)], you can use Mpgo.exe to optimize [!INCLUDE[win8_appname_long](../../../includes/win8-appname-long-md.md)] apps as well as desktop apps.</span></span>

### <a name="parallel-computing"></a><span data-ttu-id="fdea9-910">并行计算</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-910">Parallel computing</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-911">[!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] 提供了针对并行计算的多项新功能和改进功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-911">The [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] provides several new features and improvements for parallel computing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-912">其中包括改进的性能、增强的控件、对异步编程的增强支持、新的数据流库以及对并行调试和性能分析的增强支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-912">These include improved performance, increased control, improved support for asynchronous programming, a new dataflow library, and improved support for parallel debugging and performance analysis.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-913">请参阅“使用 .NET 进行并行编程”博客中的 [.NET 4.5 中有关并行的新增功能](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=235061)条目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-913">See the entry [What’s New for Parallelism in .NET 4.5](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=235061) in the Parallel Programming with .NET blog.</span></span>

<a name="networking"></a> 
### <a name="networking"></a><span data-ttu-id="fdea9-919">网络</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-919">Networking</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-920">[!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] 提供了一个用于 HTTP 应用程序的新编程接口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-920">The [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] provides a new programming interface for HTTP applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-921">有关详细信息，请参阅新的 <xref:System.Net.Http?displayProperty=nameWithType> 和 <xref:System.Net.Http.Headers?displayProperty=nameWithType> 命名空间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-921">For more information, see the new <xref:System.Net.Http?displayProperty=nameWithType> and <xref:System.Net.Http.Headers?displayProperty=nameWithType> namespaces.</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-922">还包含针对用于接受 WebSocket 连接并与之交互（通过使用现有 <xref:System.Net.HttpListener> 和相关类）的新编程接口的支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-922">Support is also included for a new programming interface for accepting and interacting with a WebSocket connection by using the existing <xref:System.Net.HttpListener> and related classes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-923">有关详细信息，请参阅新的 <xref:System.Net.WebSockets> 命名空间和 <xref:System.Net.HttpListener> 类。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-923">For more information, see the new <xref:System.Net.WebSockets> namespace and the <xref:System.Net.HttpListener> class.</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-924">此外，[!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] 包括以下网络改进：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-924">In addition, the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] includes the following networking improvements:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-925">与 RFC 兼容的 URI 支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-925">RFC-compliant URI support.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-926">有关详细信息，请参阅 <xref:System.Uri> 和相关类。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-926">For more information, see <xref:System.Uri> and related classes.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-927">对国际域名 (IDN) 分析的支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-927">Support for Internationalized Domain Name (IDN) parsing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-928">有关详细信息，请参阅 <xref:System.Uri> 和相关类。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-928">For more information, see <xref:System.Uri> and related classes.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-929">对电子邮件地址国际化 (EAI) 的支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-929">Support for Email Address Internationalization (EAI).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-930">有关更多信息，请参见 <xref:System.Net.Mail> 命名空间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-930">For more information, see the <xref:System.Net.Mail> namespace.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-931">改进的 IPv6 支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-931">Improved IPv6 support.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-932">有关更多信息，请参见 <xref:System.Net.NetworkInformation> 命名空间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-932">For more information, see the <xref:System.Net.NetworkInformation> namespace.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-933">双重模式套接字支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-933">Dual-mode socket support.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-934">有关更多信息，请参见 <xref:System.Net.Sockets.Socket> 和 <xref:System.Net.Sockets.TcpListener> 类。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-934">For more information, see the <xref:System.Net.Sockets.Socket> and <xref:System.Net.Sockets.TcpListener> classes.</span></span>

<a name="client"></a> 
### <a name="windows-presentation-foundation-wpf"></a><span data-ttu-id="fdea9-935">Windows Presentation Foundation (WPF)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-935">Windows Presentation Foundation (WPF)</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-936">在 [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] 中，Windows Presentation Foundation (WPF) 包含以下方面的更改和改进：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-936">In the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)], Windows Presentation Foundation (WPF) contains changes and improvements in the following areas:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-937">利用新的 <xref:System.Windows.Controls.Ribbon.Ribbon> 控件，你可以实现承载快速访问工具栏、应用程序菜单和选项卡的功能区用户界面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-937">The new <xref:System.Windows.Controls.Ribbon.Ribbon> control, which enables you to implement a ribbon user interface that hosts a Quick Access Toolbar, Application Menu, and tabs.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-938">支持同步和异步数据验证的新 <xref:System.ComponentModel.INotifyDataErrorInfo> 接口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-938">The new <xref:System.ComponentModel.INotifyDataErrorInfo> interface, which supports synchronous and asynchronous data validation.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-939"><xref:System.Windows.Controls.VirtualizingPanel> 和 <xref:System.Windows.Threading.Dispatcher> 类的新功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-939">New features for the <xref:System.Windows.Controls.VirtualizingPanel> and <xref:System.Windows.Threading.Dispatcher> classes.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-940">通过在非 UI 线程上访问集合，改进了在显示大型分组数据集时的性能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-940">Improved performance when displaying large sets of grouped data, and by accessing collections on non-UI threads.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-941">针对静态属性的数据绑定、针对实现 <xref:System.Reflection.ICustomTypeProvider> 接口的自定义类型的数据绑定，以及从绑定表达式中检索数据绑定信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-941">Data binding to static properties, data binding to custom types that implement the <xref:System.Reflection.ICustomTypeProvider> interface, and retrieval of data binding information from a binding expression.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-942">在值发生更改时重新定位数据（实时数据整理）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-942">Repositioning of data as the values change (live shaping).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-943">能够检查项目容器的数据上下文是否已断开连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-943">Ability to check whether the data context for an item container is disconnected.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-944">能够设置属性更改和数据源更新之间的时间间隔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-944">Ability to set the amount of time that should elapse between property changes and data source updates.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-945">改进了对实现弱事件模式的支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-945">Improved support for implementing weak event patterns.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-946">此外，事件现在可以接受标记扩展。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-946">Also, events can now accept markup extensions.</span></span>

<a name="windows_communication_foundation"></a> 
### <a name="windows-communication-foundation-wcf"></a><span data-ttu-id="fdea9-947">Windows Communication Foundation (WCF)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-947">Windows Communication Foundation (WCF)</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-948">在 [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] 中，已添加以下功能，以便更轻松地编写和维护 Windows Communication Foundation (WCF) 应用程序：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-948">In the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)], the following features have been added to make it simpler to write and maintain Windows Communication Foundation (WCF) applications:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-949">简化生成的配置文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-949">Simplification of generated configuration files.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-950">对协定优先开发的支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-950">Support for contract-first development.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-951">能够更轻松地配置 ASP.NET 兼容模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-951">Ability to configure ASP.NET compatibility mode more easily.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-952">对默认传输属性值的更改，可减小你必须设置这些值的可能性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-952">Changes in default transport property values to reduce the likelihood that you will have to set them.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-953">对 <xref:System.Xml.XmlDictionaryReaderQuotas> 类进行更新，可减小你必须手动为 XML 字典读取器配置配额的可能性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-953">Updates to the <xref:System.Xml.XmlDictionaryReaderQuotas> class to reduce the likelihood that you will have to manually configure quotas for XML dictionary readers.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-954">作为生成过程的一部分，由 Visual Studio 验证 WCF 配置文件，以便你可以在运行应用程序之前检测配置错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-954">Validation of WCF configuration files by Visual Studio as part of the build process, so you can detect configuration errors before you run your application.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-955">新的异步流支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-955">New asynchronous streaming support.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-956">新的 HTTPS 协议映射，使你能够更轻松地通过 Internet Information Services (IIS) 在 HTTPS 上公开终结点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-956">New HTTPS protocol mapping to make it easier to expose an endpoint over HTTPS with Internet Information Services (IIS).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-957">能够通过将 `?singleWSDL` 追加到服务 URL，来在单个 WSDL 文档中生成元数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-957">Ability to generate metadata in a single WSDL document by appending `?singleWSDL` to the service URL.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-958">WebSockets 支持，通过端口 80 和 443 启用真正的双向通信，其性能特性与 TCP 传输类似。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-958">Websockets support to enable true bidirectional communication over ports 80 and 443 with performance characteristics similar to the TCP transport.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-959">对在代码中配置服务的支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-959">Support for configuring services in code.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-960">XML 编辑器工具提示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-960">XML Editor tooltips.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-961"><xref:System.ServiceModel.ChannelFactory> 缓存支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-961"><xref:System.ServiceModel.ChannelFactory> caching support.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-962">二进制文件编码器压缩支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-962">Binary encoder compression support.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-963">对 UDP 传输的支持，这可使开发人员编写使用“发后不理”消息的服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-963">Support for a UDP transport that enables developers to write services that use "fire and forget" messaging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-964">客户端向服务发送消息，且不希望从该服务获得响应。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-964">A client sends a message to a service and expects no response from the service.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-965">能够在使用 HTTP 传输和传输安全性时，支持单个 WCF 终结点上的多个身份验证模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-965">Ability to support multiple authentication modes on a single WCF endpoint when using the HTTP transport and transport security.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-966">对使用国际域名 (IDN) 的 WCF 服务的支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-966">Support for WCF services that use internationalized domain names (IDNs).</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-967">有关详细信息，请参阅 [Windows Communication Foundation 中的新增功能](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=228173)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-967">For more information, see [What's New in Windows Communication Foundation](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=228173).</span></span>

<a name="windows_workflow_foundation"></a> 
### <a name="windows-workflow-foundation-wf"></a><span data-ttu-id="fdea9-968">Windows Workflow Foundation (WF)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-968">Windows Workflow Foundation (WF)</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-969">在 [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] 中，已将几项新功能添加到 Windows Workflow Foundation (WF) 中，包括：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-969">In the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)], several new features were added to Windows Workflow Foundation (WF), including:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-970">首次作为 .NET Framework 4.0.1（[.NET Framework 4 平台更新 1](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=215092)）的一部分引入的状态机工作流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-970">State machine workflows, which were first introduced as part of the .NET Framework 4.0.1 ([.NET Framework 4 Platform Update 1](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=215092)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-971">此更新包括可使开发人员创建状态机工作流的多个新类和活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-971">This update included several new classes and activities that enabled developers to create state machine workflows.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-972">已针对 [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] 更新这些类和活动以包含：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-972">These classes and activities were updated for the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] to include:</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-973">对状态设置断点的能力。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-973">The ability to set breakpoints on states.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-974">在工作流设计器中复制和粘贴转换的能力。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-974">The ability to copy and paste transitions in the workflow designer.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-975">对共享的触发器转换创建的设计器支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-975">Designer support for shared trigger transition creation.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-976">创建状态机工作流的活动，包括：<xref:System.Activities.Statements.StateMachine>、<xref:System.Activities.Statements.State> 和 <xref:System.Activities.Statements.Transition>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-976">Activities for creating state machine workflows, including: <xref:System.Activities.Statements.StateMachine>, <xref:System.Activities.Statements.State>, and <xref:System.Activities.Statements.Transition>.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-977">增强的工作流设计器功能如下:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-977">Enhanced Workflow Designer features such as the following:</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-978">Visual Studio 中增强的工作流搜索功能，包括“快速查找”和“在文件中查找”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-978">Enhanced workflow search capabilities in Visual Studio, including **Quick Find** and **Find in Files**.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-979">将第二个子活动添加到容器活动中时自动创建“序列”活动以及在“序列”活动中包括这两个活动的能力。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-979">Ability to automatically create a Sequence activity when a second child activity is added to a container activity, and to include both activities in the Sequence activity.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-980">平移支持，可让工作流的可见部分发生更改，而无需使用滚动条。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-980">Panning support, which enables the visible portion of a workflow to be changed without using the scroll bars.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-981">新“文档大纲”视图，它在树样式的大纲视图中显示工作流组件并允许在“文档大纲”视图中选择组件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-981">A new **Document Outline** view that shows the components of a workflow in a tree-style outline view and lets you select a component in the **Document Outline** view.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-982">向活动中添加批注的能力。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-982">Ability to add annotations to activities.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-983">通过使用工作流设计器定义和使用活动委托的能力。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-983">Ability to define and consume activity delegates by using the workflow designer.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-984">状态机和流程图工作流中活动和转换的自动连接和自动插入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-984">Auto-connect and auto-insert for activities and transitions in state machine and flowchart workflows.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-985">XAML 文件的单个元素中工作流的视图状态信息存储，以便你可以轻松定位和编辑视图状态信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-985">Storage of the view state information for a workflow in a single element in the XAML file, so you can easily locate and edit the view state information.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-986">可防止子活动持久化的 NoPersistScope 容器活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-986">A NoPersistScope container activity to prevent child activities from persisting.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-987">对 C# 表达式的支持：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-987">Support for C# expressions:</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-988">使用 Visual Basic 的工作流项目将使用 Visual Basic 表达式，C# 工作流项目将使用 C# 表达式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-988">Workflow projects that use Visual Basic will use Visual Basic expressions, and C# workflow projects will use C# expressions.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-989">在 Visual Studio 2010 中创建并具有 Visual Basic 表达式的 C# 工作流项目与使用 C# 表达式的 C# 工作流项目兼容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-989">C# workflow projects that were created in Visual Studio 2010 and that have Visual Basic expressions are compatible with C# workflow projects that use C# expressions.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-990">版本控制增强功能：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-990">Versioning enhancements:</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-991">新 <xref:System.Activities.WorkflowIdentity> 类，它提供了保留的工作流实例与其工作流定义之间的映射。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-991">The new  <xref:System.Activities.WorkflowIdentity> class, which provides a mapping between a persisted workflow instance and its workflow definition.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-992">同一主机中多个工作流版本的并行执行，包括 <xref:System.ServiceModel.Activities.WorkflowServiceHost>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-992">Side-by-side execution of multiple workflow versions in the same host, including <xref:System.ServiceModel.Activities.WorkflowServiceHost>.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-993">在动态更新中，修改保留的工作流实例的定义的能力。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-993">In Dynamic Update, the ability to modify the definition of a persisted workflow instance.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-994">协定优先工作流服务开发，它为自动生成活动以匹配现有服务协定提供支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-994">Contract-first workflow service development, which provides support for automatically generating activities to match an existing service contract.</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-995">有关详细信息，请参阅 [Windows Workflow Foundation 中的新增功能](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=228176)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-995">For more information, see [What's New in Windows Workflow Foundation](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=228176).</span></span>

<a name="tailored"></a> 
### [!INCLUDE[net_win8_profile](../../../includes/net-win8-profile-md.md)]
 [!INCLUDE[win8_appname_long](../../../includes/win8-appname-long-md.md)]<span data-ttu-id="fdea9-996">应用程序为特定窗体因素而设计，并利用 Windows 操作系统的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-996"> apps are designed for specific form factors and leverage the power of the Windows operating system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-997">通过使用 C# 或 Visual Basic，[!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] 或 4.5.1 的子集可用于生成面向 Windows 的 [!INCLUDE[win8_appname_long](../../../includes/win8-appname-long-md.md)]应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-997">A subset of the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] or 4.5.1 is available for building [!INCLUDE[win8_appname_long](../../../includes/win8-appname-long-md.md)] apps for Windows by using C# or Visual Basic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-998">该子集称为 [!INCLUDE[net_win8_profile](../../../includes/net-win8-profile-md.md)]，在 Windows 开发人员中心的[概述](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=228491)中进行讨论。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-998">This subset is called [!INCLUDE[net_win8_profile](../../../includes/net-win8-profile-md.md)] and is discussed in an [overview](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=228491) in the Windows Dev Center.</span></span>

<a name="portable"></a> 
### <a name="portable-class-libraries"></a><span data-ttu-id="fdea9-999">可移植类库</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-999">Portable Class Libraries</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-1000">利用 [!INCLUDE[vs_dev11_long](../../../includes/vs-dev11-long-md.md)]（和更高版本）中的可移植类库项目，你可以编写和生成在多个 .NET Framework 平台上运行的托管程序集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-1000">The Portable Class Library project in [!INCLUDE[vs_dev11_long](../../../includes/vs-dev11-long-md.md)] (and later versions) enables you to write and build managed assemblies that work on multiple .NET Framework platforms.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-1001">使用可移植类库项目，你可以选择要作为目标的平台（如 Windows Phone 和[!INCLUDE[net_win8_profile](../../../includes/net-win8-profile-md.md)]）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-1001">Using a Portable Class Library project, you choose the platforms (such as Windows Phone and [!INCLUDE[net_win8_profile](../../../includes/net-win8-profile-md.md)]) to target.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-1002">项目中的可用类型和成员自动限制为这些平台中的公共类型和成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-1002">The available types and members in your project are automatically restricted to the common types and members across these platforms.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="fdea9-1003">有关详细信息，请参阅[可移植类库](../../../docs/standard/cross-platform/cross-platform-development-with-the-portable-class-library.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="fdea9-1003">For more information, see [Portable Class Library](../../../docs/standard/cross-platform/cross-platform-development-with-the-portable-class-library.md).</span></span>
